It features Helly Tech Professional technology for extreme waterproofing and breathability, perfect for harsh conditions. With PrimaLoft LIFALOFT insulation, LIFE POCKET, SKI FREE, and other convenient features, it's suitable for various winter pursuits like resort skiing, freeriding, and mountaineering.
